defined_text = { #
	name = PRESIDENT_POLL_SLOT_1
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.aip_support > USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.gop_support
            }
			check_variable = {
				USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.aip_support > USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.dem_support
			}
			check_variable = { USA.show_usa_congress_alt_3_way = 1 }
		}
		localization_key = "Byrd: [?USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.aip_support|2]%"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.dem_support > USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.gop_support
            }
			check_variable = {
				USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.dem_support > USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.aip_support
			}
			check_variable = { USA.show_usa_congress_alt_3_way = 1 }
		}
		localization_key = "Stevenson: [?USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.dem_support|2]%"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.dem_support < USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.gop_support
            }
			check_variable = {
				 USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.aip_support < USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.gop_support
			}
			check_variable = { USA.show_usa_congress_alt_3_way = 1 }
		}
		localization_key = "Eisenhower: [?USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.gop_support|2]%"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.dem_support > USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.gop_support
            }
			check_variable = { USA.show_usa_congress_alt_3_way = 0 }
		}
		localization_key = "Stevenson: [?USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.dem_support|2]%"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.dem_support < USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.gop_support
            }
			check_variable = { USA.show_usa_congress_alt_3_way = 0 }
		}
		localization_key = "Eisenhower: [?USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.gop_support|2]%"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.dem_support = USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.gop_support
            }
			check_variable = { USA.show_usa_congress_alt_3_way = 0 }
		}
		localization_key = "Stevenson: 50%"
	}
}
defined_text = { #
	name = PRESIDENT_POLL_SLOT_2
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = {
					USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.aip_support < USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.gop_support
				}
				check_variable = {
					USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.aip_support < USA_SEN_MAP_TARGET.dem_support
				}
			}
			OR = {

defined_text = { #
	name = SPEAKER_TITLE
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA.gop_house_caucus > USA.dem_house_caucus
            }
            date < 1959.1.3
		}
		localization_key = "Joseph Martin"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA.gop_house_caucus > USA.dem_house_caucus
            }
            date > 1959.1.2
            date < 1965.1.3
		}
		localization_key = "Charles Halleck"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA.gop_house_caucus > USA.dem_house_caucus
            }
            date > 1965.1.2
            date < 1973.12.6
		}
		localization_key = "Gerald Ford"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA.gop_house_caucus > USA.dem_house_caucus
            }
            date > 1973.12.5
            date < 1981.1.3
		}
		localization_key = "John Jacob Rhodes Jr."
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA.gop_house_caucus > USA.dem_house_caucus
            }
            date > 1981.1.2
		}
		localization_key = "Robert Michel"
	}
    #Democratic Speakers
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA.dem_house_caucus > USA.gop_house_caucus
            }
            date < 1961.16.1
		}
		localization_key = "Sam Rayburn"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA.dem_house_caucus > USA.gop_house_caucus
            }
            date > 1961.15.1
            date < 1971.1.3
		}
		localization_key = "John McCormack"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA.dem_house_caucus > USA.gop_house_caucus
            }
            date > 1971.1.2
            date < 1977.1.3
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = president_albert
            }
		}
		localization_key = "Carl Albert"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                USA.dem_house_caucus > USA.gop_house_caucus
            }
            OR = {
                has_country_flag = president_albert
                date > 1977.1.2
            }
		}
		localization_key = "Tip O'Neill"
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = AlgeriaConflictStartDesc
	text = {
		trigger = {
            has_country_flag = Oran_Operation
		}
		localization_key = ALGERIA_WAR_START_DESC_ORAN
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            has_country_flag = Constatine_Operation
		}
		localization_key = ALGERIA_WAR_START_DESC_CONSTATINE
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
            has_country_flag = Bouira_Operation
		}
		localization_key = ALGERIA_WAR_START_DESC_BOUIRA
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = AlgeriaConflictTitle
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                FRA.current_inflicted_casualties_on_@ALG = ALG.current_inflicted_casualties_on_@FRA
            }
		}
		localization_key = "Inconclusive Operation"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = ALG
            check_variable = {
                FRA.current_inflicted_casualties_on_@ALG < ALG.current_inflicted_casualties_on_@FRA
            }
		}
		localization_key = "Successful Operation"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = FRA
            check_variable = {
                FRA.current_inflicted_casualties_on_@ALG > ALG.current_inflicted_casualties_on_@FRA
            }
		}
		localization_key = "Successful Operation"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = ALG
            check_variable = {
                FRA.current_inflicted_casualties_on_@ALG > ALG.current_inflicted_casualties_on_@FRA
            }
		}
		localization_key = "Failed Operation"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = FRA
            check_variable = {
                FRA.current_inflicted_casualties_on_@ALG < ALG.current_inflicted_casualties_on_@FRA
            }
		}
		localization_key = "Failed Operation"
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = BCPConflictDesc
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                BCP.Communist_Conflict_Strength = BRM.Communist_Conflict_Strength
            }
		}
		localization_key = BCP_DESC1
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = BCP
            check_variable = {
                BCP.Communist_Conflict_Strength > BRM.Communist_Conflict_Strength
            }
		}
		localization_key = BCP_DESC3
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = BRM
            check_variable = {
                BCP.Communist_Conflict_Strength < BRM.Communist_Conflict_Strength
            }
		}
		localization_key = BCP_DESC2
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = BCP
            check_variable = {
                BCP.Communist_Conflict_Strength < BRM.Communist_Conflict_Strength
            }
		}
		localization_key = BCP_DESC2
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = BRM
            check_variable = {
                BCP.Communist_Conflict_Strength > BRM.Communist_Conflict_Strength
            }
		}
		localization_key = BCP_DESC3
	}
}
defined_text = {
	name = BCPConflictTitle
	text = {
		trigger = {
            check_variable = {
                BCP.Communist_Conflict_Strength = BRM.Communist_Conflict_Strength
            }
		}
		localization_key = "Inconclusive Operation"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = BCP
            check_variable = {
                BCP.Communist_Conflict_Strength > BRM.Communist_Conflict_Strength
            }
		}
		localization_key = "Successful Operation"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = BRM
            check_variable = {
                BCP.Communist_Conflict_Strength < BRM.Communist_Conflict_Strength
            }
		}
		localization_key = "Successful Operation"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = BCP
            check_variable = {
                BCP.Communist_Conflict_Strength < BRM.Communist_Conflict_Strength
            }
		}
		localization_key = "Failed Operation"
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			tag = BRM
            check_variable = {
                BCP.Communist_Conflict_Strength > BRM.Communist_Conflict_Strength
            }
		}
		localization_key = "Failed Operation"
	}
}

	}

defined_text = {
   name = MorroccoProtectorateStatusDesc
	text = {
	   trigger = {
		   tag = SPR
	   }
	   localization_key = "Spanish rule in Morocco began in the early twentieth century when Spain and France divided the country into separate spheres of influence. The 1920s saw Spain embroiled in the Rif War, which they won only after suffering heavy casualties. The Spanish Civil War saw Moroccan soldiers serve Spanish dictator Francisco Franco loyally. After his victory, Franco rewarded the territory with liberal policies. Moroccan nationalist parties emerged and began publicly pushing for independence. The Tangier Speech by Sultan Muhammad V called for decolonization and independence. Although indirectly focused on the French, many Moroccans in the Spanish territory were also inspired, spurring more nationalist unrest. General Rafael Garcia Valino must decide how to mobilize local support to maintain Spanish control in the face of rising nationalist unrest or prepare for a dignified Spanish exit."
	}
	text = {
	   trigger = {
			 tag = FRA
	   }
	   localization_key = "France established a protectorate over Morocco in 1912 with the Treaty of Fez. The French protectorate led to new development projects and education advancements. Moroccan soldiers played a major role in both World Wars for the French state. However, the French occupation also sparked a series of revolts and unrest. The Moroccan nationalist parties began emerging in the 1930s, launching a non-violent movement for independence. Hopes for independence after World War II were dashed, leading to increasing violence by nationalist activists. The Tangier Speech by Sultan Muhammad V called for decolonization and independence. The aftermath saw several massacres conducted by French forces in Casablanca. Tensions are high as Moroccans increasingly view armed resistance as the only means forward. General Alphonse Juin must decide how to maintain French control in spite of rising nationalist unrest or prepare for a dignified French exit from the region."
	}
	text = {
	   trigger = {
			tag = MOR
	   }
	   localization_key = "France established a protectorate over Morocco in 1912 with the Treaty of Fez. The French protectorate led to new development projects and education advancements. The Moroccan nationalist parties began emerging in the 1930s, launching a non-violent movement for independence. Hopes for independence after World War II were dashed, leading to increasing violence by nationalist activists. The Tangier Speech by Sultan Muhammad V called for decolonization and independence. The aftermath saw several massacres conducted by French forces in Casablanca. Tensions are high as Moroccans increasingly view armed resistance as the only means forward.
